0                                   5566             +*/*     BY IEAVTRT2 AND IEAVTAS1                                     */
                                    5567             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    5568             +*/* POINTED TO BY:                                                   */
                                    5569             +*/*     REGISTER 1 UPON ENTRY TO AN FRR, REGISTER 1 UPON ENTRY TO    */
                                    5570             +*/*     AN ESTAE-TYPE RECOVERY ROUTINE IF REGISTER 0 DOES NOT        */
                                    5571             +*/*     CONTAIN 12 (X'0C').                                          */
                                    5572             +*/*     ADJACENT TO EACH SUPER FRR STACK (GLOBAL SDWA)               */
                                    5573             +*/*     RT1WRTCA FIELD OF THE RT1W DATA AREA                         */
                                    5574             +*/*     RTM2RTCA AND RTM2SDW2 FIELD OF THE RTM2WA DATA AREA          */
                                    5575             +*/*     FOR TASK MODE SDWAS                                          */
                                    5576             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    5577             +*/* SERIALIZATION:                                                   */
                                    5578             +*/*     GLOBAL SDWA - PHYSICALLY DISABLED OR GLOBALLY LOCKED         */
                                    5579             +*/*     GETMAINED SDWA - SRB MODE, LOCALLY LOCKED, OR NONE           */
                                    5580             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    5581             +*/* FUNCTION:                                                        */
                                    5582             +*/*     THE SDWA PROVIDES FOR COMMUNICATION BETWEEN THE RTM AND      */
                                    5583             +*/*     FRRS OR ESTAE-TYPE RECOVERY ROUTINES.  IT CONTAINS DATA      */
                                    5584             +*/*     ABOUT THE ORIGINAL ERROR AND ALSO CONCERNING ACTIONS         */
                                    5585             +*/*     OF PREVIOUSLY ENTERED RECOVERY ROUTINES.  THE SDWA IS        */
                                    5586             +*/*     ALSO KNOWN AS THE RTCA.                                      */
                                    5587             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    5588             +*/*     THE SDWA IS USED FOR RECORDING ERRORS IN LOGREC              */
                                    5589             +*/*     AS SOFTWARE RECORDS.                                         */
                                    5590             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    5591             +*/* METHOD OF ACCESS:                                                */
                                    5592             +*/* ASM:                                                             */
                                    5593             +*/*             IHASDWA DSECT=YES,VRAMAP=YES                 @G81EP11*/
                                    5594             +*/*                           NO         NO                  @G81EP11*/
                                    5595             +*/* DSECT = YES IS THE DEFAULT AND WILL PRODUCE THE SDWA             */
                                    5596             +*/*            AS A DSECT.                                           */
                                    5597             +*/* DSECT = NO WILL PRODUCE THE SDWA AS A CONTINUATION OF            */
                                    5598             +*/*            DEFINED STORAGE. (NO DSECT CARD PRODUCED)             */
                                    5599             +*/* VRAMAP=YES IS THE DEFAULT AND WILL PRODUCE THE IHAVRA    @G81EP11*/
                                    5600             +*/*            MAPPING MACRO FIELDS FOLLOWING THE SDWA       @G81EP11*/
                                    5601             +*/*            FIELDS.                                       @G81EP11*/
                                    5602             +*/* VRAMAP=NO  WILL PRODUCE THE SDWA, BUT NOT THE IHAVRA     @G81EP11*/
                                    5603             +*/*            MAPPING MACRO.                                @G81EP11*/
                                    5604             +*/* PL/AS:                                                           */
                                    5605             +*/*   IF MACRO VARIABLE                                              */
                                    5606             +*/*   %SDWALVL IS NULL, THE SDWA WILL BE INCLUDED                    */
                                    5607             +*/*   AS A LEVEL 1 STRUCTURE BASED ON SDWAPTR.                       */
                                    5608             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    5609             +*/*   IF %SDWALVL IS SPECIFIED AS A NUMBER FROM 1 TO 4               */
                                    5610             +*/*   THE SDWA WILL BE A NON-BASED STRUCTURE WITH THE                */
                                    5611             +*/*   TOP LEVEL EQUAL TO %SDWALVL.                                   */
                                    5612             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    5613             +*/*   THE DEFAULT INCLUSION OF THE IHAVRA MAPPING MACRO      @G81EP11*/
                                    5614             +*/*   ALONG WITH THE SDWA CAN BE SUPPRESSED BY SETTING       @G81EP11*/
                                    5615             +*/*   MACRO VARIABLE SDWAVRAMAP EQUAL TO 'NO'.               @G81EP11*/
                                    5616             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    5617             +*/*   VIA ATTRIBUTE - SPECIFY %IHAVIA='YES' BEFORE %INCLUDE.         */
                                    5618             +*/*                   DECLARE SDWAALET.                              */
                                    5619             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    5620             +*/*   Note: In order to access SDWARC4, that DSECT must be based     */
                                    5621             +*/*         upon SDWAXEME.  See the SDWARC4 section for details. @LIA*/

0                                   5622             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    5623             +*/* DEPENDENCIES =                                                   */
                                    5624             +*/*                CHANGES TO THE SIZE OF THIS MACRO REQUIRE A NEW   */
                                    5625             +*/*                VERSION NUMBER.  WHEN THE SIZE OF THIS MACRO IS   */
                                    5626             +*/*                CHANGED, IT MUST BE DONE IN DOUBLE WORD           */
                                    5627             +*/*                INCREMENTS.  SIZE CHANGES TO THE SDWA ARE         */
                                    5628             +*/*                REFLECTED IN IHART1W.  MODULES THAT USE EITHER    */
                                    5629             +*/*                MACRO TO GET OR RELEASE SDWA STORAGE MUST BE      */
                                    5630             +*/*                RECOMPILED.  ALSO, IHASFPL MUST BE UPDATED TO     */
                                    5631             +*/*                MATCH THE NEW VERSION AND ITS ASSOCIATED MODULES  */
                                    5632             +*/*                MUST BE RECOMPILED.                               */
                                    5633             +*/*                THE HARD CODED VALUES IN WSACSTKA AND WSACSTKB    */
                                    5634             +*/*                IN THE IHAWSAVT MACRO MUST BE UPDATED, AND ANY    */
                                    5635             +*/*                MODULES THAT USE THOSE FIELDS SHOULD BE           */
                                    5636             +*/*                RECOMPILED.                                   @P6C*/
                                    5637             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    5638             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    5639             +*/* USAGE =                                                          */
                                    5640             +*/*     THE SDWA HAS EXTENSIONS.  THE SDWAXPAD (X'170') POINTS TO    */
                                    5641             +*/*     AN EXTENSION WHICH IS MADE UP OF POINTERS TO ALL THE OTHER   */
                                    5642             +*/*     EXTENSIONS.  THE MAIN BODY AND POINTERS EXTENSION WILL       */
                                    5643             +*/*     ALWAYS EXIST WHILE THE OTHER EXTENSIONS MAY NOT DEPENDING    */
                                    5644             +*/*     ON THE ERROR ENVIRONMENT.  PHYSICALLY, THE MAIN BODY OF THE  */
                                    5645             +*/*     SDWA COMES FIRST, FOLLOWED BY THE RECORDABLE EXTENSIONS,     */
                                    5646             +*/*     THEN THE POINTERS EXTENSION, AND LAST THE NON-RECORDABLE     */
                                    5647             +*/*     EXTENSIONS.                                                  */
                                    5648             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    5649             +*/*                   ***************                                */
                                    5650             +*/*                   *             *                                */
                                    5651             +*/*                   *    SDWA     *                                */
                                    5652             +*/*                   *             *                                */
                                    5653             +*/*                   ***************                                */
                                    5654             +*/*                   *  SDWARC1    *                                */
                                    5655             +*/*                   ***************                                */
                                    5656             +*/*                   *  SDWARC2    *                                */
                                    5657             +*/*                   ***************                                */
                                    5658             +*/*                   *  SDWARC3    *                                */
                                    5659             +*/*                   ***************                                */
                                    5660             +*/*                   *  SDWARC4    *                            @LIA*/
                                    5661             +*/*                   ***************                                */
                                    5662             +*/*                   *  SDWAPTRS   *                                */
                                    5663             +*/*                   *  --------   *                                */
                                    5664             +*/*                   *    ORDER    *                                */
                                    5665             +*/*                   * => SDWANRC1 *                                */
                                    5666             +*/*                   * => SDWARC1  *                                */
                                    5667             +*/*                   * => SDWARC2  *                                */
                                    5668             +*/*                   * => SDWANRC2 *                            @01C*/
                                    5669             +*/*                   * => SDWARC3  *                            @01C*/
                                    5670             +*/*                   * => SDWANRC3 *                            @L7A*/
                                    5671             +*/*                   * => SDWARC4  *                            @LIA*/
                                    5672             +*/*                   ***************                                */
                                    5673             +*/*                   *  SDWANRC1   *                                */
                                    5674             +*/*                   ***************                                */
                                    5675             +*/*                   *  SDWANRC2   *                                */
                                    5676             +*/*                   ***************                            @L1C*/
                                    5677             +*/*                   *  SDWANRC3   *                                */

                                    6789             +*/*  Macro Name: IHAVRA                                              */
                                    6790             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    6791             +*/*  Dsect Name: VRAMAP                                              */
                                    6792             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    6793             +*/*  Descriptive Name: Variable Recording Area                       */
                                    6794             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    6795             +*/* COPYRIGHT:                                                       */
                                    6796             +*/*     5645-001                                                 @P3C*/
                                    6797             +*/*     THIS MODULE IS "RESTRICTED MATERIALS OF IBM"                 */
                                    6798             +*/*     (C) COPYRIGHT IBM CORP. 1981, 1996                       @P3C*/
                                    6799             +*/*     LICENSED MATERIALS - PROPERTY OF IBM                         */
                                    6800             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    6801             +*/*  STATUS: HBB6601                                             @P3C*/
                                    6802             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    6803             +*/*  Component: RTM (SCRTM)                                      @P3C*/
                                    6804             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    6805             +*/*  External Classification: GUPI                                   */
                                    6806             +*/*  End of External Classification: GUPI                            */
                                    6807             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    6808             +*/*  Storage attributes:                                             */
                                    6809             +*/*    Subpool: Same as containing structure                         */
                                    6810             +*/*    Key:     Same as containing structure                         */
                                    6811             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    6812             +*/*  Function:                                                       */
                                    6813             +*/*     Maps the SDWA Variable Recording Area (SDWAVRA) or a         */
                                    6814             +*/*     component-maintained area in a key, length, data format,     */
                                    6815             +*/*     to speed up error analysis. Also provides constants for      */
                                    6816             +*/*     SDWA data and for ABDUMP symptom data.                       */
                                    6817             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    6818             +*/*01*  Keys are provided to indicate symptom data from the          */
                                    6819             +*/*     following sources:                                           */
                                    6820             +*/*       - SDWA fixed areas, including extensions.                  */
                                    6821             +*/*       - SDWAVRA.                                                 */
                                    6822             +*/*       - ABDUMP symptom area (see AMDDATA macro, structure        */
                                    6823             +*/*                PRDSYSMD)                                         */
                                    6824             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    6825             +*/*     Examples of component-maintained areas are SDUMP 4K          */
                                    6826             +*/*     buffer and the LRB control block user data field,            */
                                    6827             +*/*     LRBTUSR, for wait state data.                                */
                                    6828             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    6829             +*/*  Usage:                                                          */
                                    6830             +*/*     Any recovery routine or other error handling routine can     */
                                    6831             +*/*     use this mapping to create formatted error information       */
                                    6832             +*/*     within the SDWAVRA or in other (component-maintained) areas. */
                                    6833             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    6834             +*/*     The SDWAVRAM bit must be turned on if the SDWAVRA data is    */
                                    6835             +*/*     mapped.  Also, users of the SDWAVRA must set the SDWAURAL    */
                                    6836             +*/*     field equal to the length of the user-supplied data.         */
                                    6837             +*/*                                                                  */
                                    6838             +*/*     The VRADATA executable macro can be used to reduce the       */
                                    6839             +*/*     lines of code required to put data in a key, length, data    */
                                    6840             +*/*     format.  Use the VRAINIT keyword to set the SDWAVRAM bit     */
                                    6841             +*/*     and respecify VRAMAP based on VRAPTR.                        */
